  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_cee23795-62a1-4b4e-840b-5833c64790c0'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer730098264" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14518627568910843406"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380747943ra/3118894.gif' alt=' photo what.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Okay let me start by saying that I've had the pleasure of reading great books by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4851199.Tijan' title='Tijan' rel='nofollow noopener'>Tijan</a> before. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18221931.Carter_Reed' title='Carter Reed by Tijan' rel='nofollow noopener'>Carter Reed</a> however, didn't live up to my expectations.<br/><br/><b>We're first introduced to Emma. Who happens to arrive home early one day to find her room mate being raped, by her own boyfriend.<br/>Emma only has seconds to make a decision - 1. Call the cops, and be killed by his family's mafia connections, or - 2. Kill him and hope for the best.<br/>She of course picks #2. (I probably would too)<br/>After all is said and done</b></span>
  <span id="freeText14518627568910843406" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380747943ra/3118894.gif" alt=" photo what.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Okay let me start by saying that I've had the pleasure of reading great books by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4851199.Tijan" title="Tijan" rel="nofollow noopener">Tijan</a> before. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18221931.Carter_Reed" title="Carter Reed by Tijan" rel="nofollow noopener">Carter Reed</a> however, didn't live up to my expectations.<br><br><b>We're first introduced to Emma. Who happens to arrive home early one day to find her room mate being raped, by her own boyfriend.<br>Emma only has seconds to make a decision - 1. Call the cops, and be killed by his family's mafia connections, or - 2. Kill him and hope for the best.<br>She of course picks #2. (I probably would too)<br>After all is said and done, she runs to the only person she knows (and hopes) will protect her. Carter Reed.<br>Now Carter is balls deep in the mob. He's a weapon. A very powerful one. He's also Emma's little secret.</b><br><br>Now the first half wasn't that bad! Overlooking little things that annoyed me, I enjoyed it. However after the story started progressing, I could no longer let those things slide.<br><br>Emma was the most self centred bitch I've ever had the displeasure of reading.<br>All she thought about was herself. I hate a pity party, and she was the star at that show.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380747943ra/3118895.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mssy01U2Tj1s6lhw6o1_500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She also cried WAY too much for my liking.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380747943ra/3118896.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mtsr12mvEq1sp9fcho1_500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sure, she just shot someone - She has a right to feel upset. Yes? Yes. She does. I though feel if she can sit around thinking about her vagina and wanting orgasms all day - she's not that sad. I don't know about you, but when I think of orgasms - I think of lollipops and rainbows. Ok not really. But do you see where I'm going?<br><br>Emma wasn't a good friend. She was able to keep her life somewhat together going out, working etcetera without a care in the world of what her traumatized friend was going through.<br> When she did find out however...ARRG! You know what? You read it. Hey you might even enjoy it.<br><br><br><b> Carter Reed </b>. Apart from the first chapter in the book, he actually reminded me of a big grumpy teddy bear! SO SOFT - YET SO MAD! AWW.<img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380747943ra/3118897.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mj34wiJtGD1s3qtroo1_500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>How he could stand her blubbering mess and psychotic possessive behaviour, let alone love her - Is beyond me. Everyone needs love though, so whatever.<br><br>There's so much I want to say, but I know I've rambled on a little too much that I don't make sense. So instead I'll present you with a show of gifs!<br><br><b><u> How I interpreted this story </u></b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380747943ra/3118898.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mgtxzmVbsE1ql5qkqo1_500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380436105ra/881355.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m61wyaZeWT1rqfhi2o1_400.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380747943ra/3118899.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mohrtsT9d21s64nhuo1_500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380747943ra/3118900.gif" alt=" photo swoon.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380747943ra/3118901.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mn0d9puDDq1rm49iao1_500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380747943ra/3118902.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_msvsm29YGQ1ria5seo1_500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><u> This is how I felt </u></b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380747943ra/3118903.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_moo4np1zdR1qfeafco1_500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img to the fact I did enjoy the first half of this book.</span>

<div id="review_724744831" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/724744831" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/724744831?book_show_action=true">Sep 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Christy by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer724744831" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9065620634510872850"><b>5 Carter Reed stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/577978e9-0e21-4304-85e4-3323ec569596_zps684ae7f4.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410685969i/11140282.jpg' alt=' photo 577978e9-0e21-4304-85e4-3323ec569596_zps684ae7f4.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>She’s done it again… I’ve been Tijaned a second time around. I’ve read a few of Tijan’s books and all of them have that addictive quality. Once you start reading, you don’t want to put the book down. <i>Carter Reed</i> took up my entire day. I didn’t plan on listening to an audio book for 7+ hours that evening, but I just couldn’t stop. It’s safe to say that Carter is my new favorite Tijan boy (sorry Jesse). I’ve had this book sitting on my kindle since release day and I’m so ha</span>
  <span id="freeText9065620634510872850" style="display:none"><b>5 Carter Reed stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/577978e9-0e21-4304-85e4-3323ec569596_zps684ae7f4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410685969i/11140282.jpg" alt=" photo 577978e9-0e21-4304-85e4-3323ec569596_zps684ae7f4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>She’s done it again… I’ve been Tijaned a second time around. I’ve read a few of Tijan’s books and all of them have that addictive quality. Once you start reading, you don’t want to put the book down. <i>Carter Reed</i> took up my entire day. I didn’t plan on listening to an audio book for 7+ hours that evening, but I just couldn’t stop. It’s safe to say that Carter is my new favorite Tijan boy (sorry Jesse). I’ve had this book sitting on my kindle since release day and I’m so happy I finally had the time to give it a go, but at the same time, I’m kicking myself for waiting so long!<br><br>Emma witnesses her best friend being raped. She can’t do nothing, she’s afraid the rapist will kill her friend so she kills him first. Big problem- she can’t go to the cops about it. The guy she killed has mob ties and she knows it would do no good. So she goes to a guy she hasn’t seen in ten years. Her dead brothers best friend, the one she’s supposed to trust. Carter Reed.<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“You don’t trust anyone, no one except Carter. Go to Carter. He’ll take care of you, Ems. I promise.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/3a53b4b7-10f6-4143-a027-00c2798db41b_zps8cb2a6f8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410685969i/11140283.jpg" alt=" photo 3a53b4b7-10f6-4143-a027-00c2798db41b_zps8cb2a6f8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Once I heard those words come out of Carter Reed’s mouth, I knew I was a goner. <b>I would declare war for you, Carter Reed.</b> Carter is protective. He’s a killer, yes, but once you learn about his past, you won’t really see him that way. I know I didn’t. He’s a savior . He’s loyal, he’s fierce and he’s sexy as hell. There is no way to read this book and not fall hard for Carter Reed. <br><br>Once Emma finds Carter, she finds her salvation. The road isn’t easy for these two. There is a ton of drama along the way. Emma has to give up a lot from her old life to have Carter but primarily to keep safe. That is Carter’s number one priority. Emma’s safety. It always has been. He has done and will do anything for Emma.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/da86fac4-c30f-46a1-95c2-2947ec2cc1e9_zpscd77737a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410685969i/11140284.jpg" alt=" photo da86fac4-c30f-46a1-95c2-2947ec2cc1e9_zpscd77737a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Carter Reed</i> is a suspenseful, passionate and fast paced book. It’s one that grabbed me from the beginning and didn’t let go. I loved both main characters, the story was interesting and compelling and the writing was great. Overall this was a huge win for me :D<br><br>Just a small disclaimer- before you start a Tijan book, just know that she has that ability to suck you in, make it so you don’t want to do anything else but read her book. You might not be able to stop once you start so read at your own risk. In all seriousness, <i>Carter Reed</i> is a book you won’t want to miss out on! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/f916b98a-5828-4326-9736-298e46cadef7_zps9214e0d9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410685969i/11140285.jpg" alt=" photo f916b98a-5828-4326-9736-298e46cadef7_zps9214e0d9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> </span>

<div id="review_2099232111" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2099232111" />
    <a title="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale"><img alt="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577855357p2/69106439.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2099232111?book_show_action=true">Feb 19, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" href="/user/show/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale">Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2099232111" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11152693276854363159">What do you do when your roommate and best friend is raped by her boyfriend who just happens to be the son of the local mafia boss? <br/><br/>Well, for Emma the answer is easy. She comes back from her gym class early, goes directly for her gun and shoots him. <br/>So far so good, or rather not so far and not so good. *lol*<br/><br/>*sigh* <br/>What can I say about this book? *shakes head*<br/>The first half read like an action movie and felt like <b>“Fifty Shades of Grey”</b> meets <b>the mafia</b> which actually was pretty entertaining and ke</span>
  <span id="freeText11152693276854363159" style="display:none">What do you do when your roommate and best friend is raped by her boyfriend who just happens to be the son of the local mafia boss? <br /><br />Well, for Emma the answer is easy. She comes back from her gym class early, goes directly for her gun and shoots him. <br />So far so good, or rather not so far and not so good. *lol*<br /><br />*sigh* <br />What can I say about this book? *shakes head*<br />The first half read like an action movie and felt like <b>“Fifty Shades of Grey”</b> meets <b>the mafia</b> which actually was pretty entertaining and kept the book in my good graces, but right after we hit the halfway mark the book became soo damn boring, I couldn’t even bring myself to pick it up. XD<br /><br />And that says a lot! When <b>
  <u>I</u>
</b> need an entire month for about 125 pages this means that my interest hasn’t just deserted me but also ran an extra mile to hide in the endless hills of the faerie realm. In other words: I was bored out of my mind and read everything else than <b>“Carter Reed”</b>. *lol*<br /><br />After giving this some serious thought I finally realised what didn’t work for me though. I mean it should have worked, but it didn’t so I really wanted to find out why I stopped enjoying this book. The answer is quite simple. It has an alpha male and a damsel in distress and it was supposed to be a sexy read. In the first half <b>“Carter Reed”</b> delivered exactly that, but in the second half to read on became quite strenuous. So what happened?<br /><br />The guy got the girl! <br />Yep, that’s it! Let me elaborate! ;-)<br /><br />I have no problem with alpha males or the kind of woman that’s a damsel in distress, but I have a major problem with the build-up of sexual tension and an anticlimactic release. (Oops what a choice of words. *facepalm*) Anyway! Half of the book Emma was like: “Ohhh boy Carter is so hot” and then they finally hit it off and everything goes to hell. Like excuse me but <b>WTH?!</b> All they did was to kiss each other which led to them ending up in bed. We go to the club, we party, we cry about our miserable life and lost friends and then we start all over again.<br /><br /><u>
  <b>IF THEY AT LEAST WOULD HAVE HAD THE DECENCY TO HAVE SOME FABULOUS SEX!!! *lol*</b>
</u><br /><br />But no! We don’t even get that, we get tension, tension, a kiss, a little bit of touching and groping and then it’s fade out. And this happens the rest of the entire book! Better one sex scene that is good than 20 that are bad. Where’s the point in writing such scenes when they bore you to death? *stifles a yawn*<br /><br />And where did the plot go? <br />Out of the window, as it seems!<br />What happened to the almighty mafia boss who was supposed to want revenge? If I’d be a mafia boss and someone would have killed my only heir I’d be majorly pissed, I’d like to see blood and I would find a way to get to them. But nope, Emma is untouchable because she’s Carter Reeds. Sure! Completely logical! <br />Oh and don’t even get me started on self-blaming, forever crying Emma. I just can’t!!!<br /><br />So yeah, I finally finished this book and I was actually relieved when I closed the last page. <br />The only reason <b>“Carter Reed”</b> gets 3 stars from me, is the simple fact that the book was really nice at the beginning. Unfortunately it didn’t stay that way. &gt;_&lt; I’m sorry to say it but in the end this really didn’t work out for me. <br />Not at all! <br /><br />But hey, maybe this is still the perfect read for you?!<br />Who knows? <br />As for me, I'm done with oh so shmexy Carter Reed. ;-P</span>
  <a data-text-id="11152693276854363159" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_697042133" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/697042133" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/697042133?book_show_action=true">Aug 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=standalone">standalone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=2013-release">2013-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer697042133" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8502948354481776353"><br/>♦ <b>4 PASSIONATE AND ACTION-PACKED STARS.</b> ♦<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381085876i/4138007._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>After having read a few of Tijan's previous NA series, I'd already become a fan of her work and typical writing style. So, when I read the synopsis of Carter Reed and discovered that it was going to be something very different than most of her previous work, I was very curious and anxious to find out how the story would turn out. Needless to say, my expectations were very high, and I can honestly say, the story did not disappoint. But maybe my expectation</span>
  <span id="freeText8502948354481776353" style="display:none"><br>♦ <b>4 PASSIONATE AND ACTION-PACKED STARS.</b> ♦<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381085876i/4138007._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After having read a few of Tijan's previous NA series, I'd already become a fan of her work and typical writing style. So, when I read the synopsis of Carter Reed and discovered that it was going to be something very different than most of her previous work, I was very curious and anxious to find out how the story would turn out. Needless to say, my expectations were very high, and I can honestly say, the story did not disappoint. But maybe my expectations were just a little bit too high, because I felt the storyline lacking a few times (with over dramatics and some characteristics to both of the main characters that didn't add up) and there was just something missing for me to give it a 5 star rating.<br><br>♦<br><br><b>The story starts out, quite literally, with a bang.</b><br><br>When Emma unexpectedly returns home early, she never expected her life to change as drastically as it did...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381085876i/4138008._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The moment she finds her roommate and best friend Mallory being raped by her violent jerk of a boyfriend, Jeremy Dunvan. With no other way to protect both herself and her best friend, she decides to shoot him. But, Jeremy is also the son one of the city's most vicious mafia leaders and of course his father will want to revenge his son by finding his murderer and make them suffer. Therefore Emma and Mallory have to go into hiding and leave everything they know behind.<br><br>With no one else to turn to, Emma decides to confide in the one person who might actually be able to help her out the mess her once uncomplicated life has turned into: ♦ <b>Carter Reed.</b> ♦<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381085876i/4138009.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Everyone knows Carter Reed. Or at least, evryone knows <i>of him</i>. He's a notorious member of one of the most powerful mob families in the city, or even the country. He's also known as the <b>Cold Killer.</b> With a reputation as a coldhearted, charismatic hitman who never missed his target, he is both feared and admired by a great amount of people. To Emma, Carter is an old family friend and he used to be her deceased older brothers's best friend.<br><br><i>If there's one person who can keep her safe, it's probably Carter...</i><br><br>But what happens when her supposed friends betray her trust? And when the head of Carter's rivaling mafia clan has decided to hunt her down no matter what? Will even Carter's protection be enough to keep her safe?<br><br>As the story progresses, Emma discovers just how much she really means to Carter and exactly how far he's willing to go to protect what's his...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381085876ra/4138010.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*<br><br>All in all, Carter Reed was a fun, exciting, hot and fast paced read with a lot of suspense and action. There's just something about Tijan's books that once I've started reading them, makes me want to keep reading until the very last page. Her books are addictive, easy to read and often portray strong, kick-ass heroines and bad boy heros with a soft spot in their heart that makes them irresistible. Therefore, I would highly recommend giving this story, and the rest of Tijan's books, a try! <br><br>Also worth mentioning. Carter Reed is a <i>standalone </i>with a<b> HEA.</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381085876i/4138011.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You did all that for me?"<br><br>"I would declare war for you,"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3208669023" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16483745297888978995"><b>Carter Reed is not your average book boyfriend!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1582819069i/29027999._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This was quite a book! It was definitely a wild ride from beginning to end. It was an awesome story with non-stop action. The characters were all developed very well and the world building was terrific the romance was sizzling hot. <br/><br/>This was a story about a young woman named Emma Martins who works at a hotel and lives with a friend named Mallory who makes bad choices in the men she dates. Emma comes home one night early because she decides to skip go</span>
  <span id="freeText16483745297888978995" style="display:none"><b>Carter Reed is not your average book boyfriend!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1582819069i/29027999._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was quite a book! It was definitely a wild ride from beginning to end. It was an awesome story with non-stop action. The characters were all developed very well and the world building was terrific the romance was sizzling hot. <br><br>This was a story about a young woman named Emma Martins who works at a hotel and lives with a friend named Mallory who makes bad choices in the men she dates. Emma comes home one night early because she decides to skip going to her gym. Emma finds her roommate Mallory getting brutally raped by her boyfriend, Jeremy Dunvan, who happens to be mob connected to the Bartel family.<br><br>Emma knows that Jeremy will most likely Mallory and probably her as well if he finds her in the apartment so she grabs a gun and kills him before he gets the chance. Not knowing what to do, the girls drive around until they end up at a friends place. Though Emma knows that Jeremy’s father Franco will be looking to kill her as soon as he finds out what she did.<br><br>Emma knows how dangerous Franco is since he put out a hit on her brother A.J. when they were younger and he was beaten to death with a bat right in front of her while she remained hidden behind a grate. Her brother always told her if she ever needed help to go to Carter Reed. So that is what Emma decides to do.<br><br>Emma knows, like everyone in the city that Carter Reed is a powerful mob figure in the Mauricio crime family. He has killed a lot of people to get where he is and now he owns a lot of restaurants, clubs and other businesses. So Emma goes to one of his most popular clubs to see if she can meet with him.<br><br>I won’t give away any more than that but to say that Carter Reed is quite a guy and when he takes an interest in a girl he doesn’t go half way. Emma is scared of Carter at first but she also feels safe with him which is what she needs. The action in the book is thrilling and the romance is hot. I absolutely loved it.<br><br><a href="https://www.ilikebooksbest.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a>|<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/wennel" rel="nofollow noopener">Goodreads</a>|<a href="https://www.facebook.com/ilikebooksbest" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>|<a href="https://www.instagram.com/ilikebooksbest" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a>|<a href="https://www.twitter.com/wendysu020202" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a>|<a href="https://www.bookbub.com/profile/1895823057" rel="nofollow noopener">BookBub</a></span>

<div id="review_1112356430" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1112356430" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1112356430?book_show_action=true">Nov 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Beverly by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1112356430" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7349945820761919424"><b>5 <i>Carter was lethal</i> Stars</b><br/><br/>I was having lunch with my <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/724744831?book_show_action=false&page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>bestie</a> and had told her how crazy it was that I had never read a book by Tijan. After she picked her jaw up off the floor she said, <b>“I would declare war for Carter Reed.”</b> She was completely serious and said it with such passion. After I stopped laughing I asked her what it was about. She said a mob book and brother’s best friend and I was sold. I started this audiobook in my car on the way home and was hooked. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417831729i/12556162._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The story begins with Emma witness</span>
  <span id="freeText7349945820761919424" style="display:none"><b>5 <i>Carter was lethal</i> Stars</b><br><br>I was having lunch with my <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/724744831?book_show_action=false&amp;page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">bestie</a> and had told her how crazy it was that I had never read a book by Tijan. After she picked her jaw up off the floor she said, <b>“I would declare war for Carter Reed.”</b> She was completely serious and said it with such passion. After I stopped laughing I asked her what it was about. She said a mob book and brother’s best friend and I was sold. I started this audiobook in my car on the way home and was hooked. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417831729i/12556162._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story begins with Emma witnessing her best friend being raped by her boyfriend, who also happens to be the son of a mob boss. She tries to stop things, but when that fails she is left with one option: kill or be killed. Even though Emma had the best of intentions and was heroic it leads to trouble for her. Emma and her brother were orphaned as a children, and her older brother raised her until he died. Alone, in trouble, and nowhere to go she turns to <b>Carter Reed</b>. <br><br>Carter Reed was her brother’s best friend and promised him he would take care of her if something happened to him, but Emma hasn’t seen Carter in years. Despite that she decides to go out on a limb and ask for help.<br><br>Carter Reed isn’t a regular guy, no he is a <i>made man</i> in another mob family. Carter doesn’t take prisoners, he is all in and will do anything to protect Emma. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417831729i/12556163._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>(that’s for you Chris)</i><br><br>The story is told primarily in Emma’s POV, but we do get a few scenes in Carter’s. This allows us to see what is actually going on behind the scene with the mob. This book is action packed, but still has a sexy and sweet romance. Yes, because this is Carter Reed and he is capable of being both. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417831729i/12556164._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book blew me away. There is a perfect balance of heart, action, and sexiness. There are very few books where things end I am like I wish this or I would change that - with this one there is nothing I would change. Emma had her weak moments, but for the most part this girl was fierce. I loved how she was willing to fight and die for Carter, he would never allow this, but her willingness had me loving her for Carter. Now Carter…don’t even get me started. I absolutely loved him he is sexy, protective and loving.<br><br>As if you can’t tell I loved this and highly recommend it!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13723380942689588691"><b>GUILTY PLEASURE READ AND NOTHING MORE!!! </b><br/><br/>Another addictive read by an author I can't seem to get enough of. Like I've said before, her books are my addiction, my crack, and my exception. They will always be 5-star reads for me. <br/><br/>Having said that, I will say this is my least favorite of her books (my favorite is <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17364620.Broken_and_Screwed_2__BS___2_' title='Broken and Screwed 2 (BS, #2) by Tijan' rel='nofollow noopener'>Broken and Screwed 2</a>).   <span id="freeText13723380942689588691" style="display:none"><b>GUILTY PLEASURE READ AND NOTHING MORE!!! </b><br><br>Another addictive read by an author I can't seem to get enough of. Like I've said before, her books are my addiction, my crack, and my exception. They will always be 5-star reads for me. <br><br>Having said that, I will say this is my least favorite of her books (my favorite is <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17364620.Broken_and_Screwed_2__BS___2_" title="Broken and Screwed 2 (BS, #2) by Tijan" rel="nofollow noopener">Broken and Screwed 2</a>). Tijan's plots are always a bit convoluted and disjointed, but this book took things to a whole new level. My goodness! I spent the majority of this book with what I assume was a perplexed look on my face. I couldn't for the life of me keep up with some of the random and evasive parts of the plot. This was me while reading this book. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393273016i/8685497._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Still, I can't help but give 5 stars to a book that normally would have been a 2-star read for me. As confused as I was at times, I still loved EVERY SINGLE SECOND I spent reading this addictive story. <br><br>Every reader needs a crack author and Tijan is mine. I love the feelings and emotions she evokes, even the confusing ones, when I read one of her books. The rewards outweigh the negatives for me. </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer692361107" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer12181324536672332077">Jointly reviewed for :<a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://totallybookedblog.com/'>http://totallybookedblog.com/</a><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432713i/869506._SX540_.png' width='450' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Jenny:</b> So this is the first time ever that we have marked a book to read based solely on a cover. Hey, don’t judge us. Have you seen that cover? Yep, this was one book we were dying to read and it would be an understatement to say it didn’t let us down, wouldn’t it G?<br/><br/>I absolutely LOVED Carter Reed. I was hooked from the first page and my life pretty much went on hold until I turned that last page. I was completely absorbed in every word of this </span>
  <span id="freeText12181324536672332077" style="display:none">Jointly reviewed for :<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://totallybookedblog.com/">http://totallybookedblog.com/</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432713i/869506._SX540_.png" width="450" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Jenny:</b> So this is the first time ever that we have marked a book to read based solely on a cover. Hey, don’t judge us. Have you seen that cover? Yep, this was one book we were dying to read and it would be an understatement to say it didn’t let us down, wouldn’t it G?<br><br>I absolutely LOVED Carter Reed. I was hooked from the first page and my life pretty much went on hold until I turned that last page. I was completely absorbed in every word of this author’s wonderful story. I adored her writing and she is definitely on my “to buy” list for the future! And words completely fail me about the hero Carter Reed.<br><br><b>
  <i>‘I felt like the prey being caught by the predator’ </i>
</b>– Emma<br><br>Wow! I’m devoid of speech thinking about how utterly delicious and dangerous this man was! He had such a presence and was such a force. What an amazing job this author did with this character. Every nuance, every word, every movement from this man could be felt through her prose. Needless to say I’ve met my new book boyfriend. I know you loved this one too G!<br><br><b>Gitte:</b> Oh, are we admitting to being fickle in public Jenny hahaha yes we did indeed mark this to be read, because ‘have you seen this cover??’ And then to find that the story went above and beyond that, well, wow what an absolute treat. I loved this book. I didn’t put it down unless I absolutely had to. I was completely addicted and this Author completed that fantastic hat trick with drama, passion and brilliant characters. Yeah…Carter Reed, what a man. I’m actually speechless as words fail me too when trying to describe just how perfect he is. No doubt Jenny, new book boyfriend alert!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>“I would declare war for you.”</i>
</b> – Carter<br><br><b>Jenny:</b> We’ll only briefly touch on the story because we really don’t want to give a lot away. For us, the enjoyment of this book was being surprised along the way, having our hearts racing, experiencing the suspense, the emotion and I have to say, it’s been a while since I’ve been so completely intoxicated with the sexual chemistry between two characters. Sizzling doesn’t even begin to describe it. Every look, every touch and every word between these two passionate characters made me want more!<br><br><b>
  <i>‘God, how could I want this man? He was cold, detached. He killed others.’</i>
</b> - Emma<br><br>Emma is on the run. Something went down and she’s in all sorts of trouble. The type that could get her killed. The only person she trusts is her brother’s best friend Carter Reed who has now risen through the ranks of the Mob to become one it’s most valued and dangerous members. Emma fears Carter on some levels but her brothers last words keep ringing in her head…….<br><br><b>
  <i>“You don’t trust anyone, no one except Carter. Go to Carter. He’ll take care of everything. He’ll take care of you, Ems. I promise.” </i>
</b> – AJ<br><br>Emma has had to learn to be resilient. She’s a survivor. Emma wasn’t afforded the most stable of lives and the vicious murder of her brother some years earlier still haunts her to this day. But Emma realises her only chance of survival rests in the hands of Carter Reed and so she seeks him out. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I was going to die. It was a matter of time.’</i>
</b> – Emma<br><br>And wow! This story really does take off at that point. So much unfolds and you're taken on a heart racing rollercoaster ride that's for sure! Emma remembers Carter from her younger years but he has now become a force in the Mob. Carter Reed. Where to begin to describe the strikingly handsome, cool and calculated man? Danger, sensuality and sex emanates from every pore of Carter Reed. This man is feared and respected, yet he does have one weakness and that is Emma. Gitte, you really did feel every intense, passionate and emotional moment that passed between Emma and Carter didn’t you?<br><br><b>Gitte: </b> I agree Jenny, it would be such a shame for this story to be spoilt for readers as the build-up and pacing is brilliant. The seductive passion, angst, drama and intrigue is palpable. I was so invested from the start, and not having any idea where this story was going to go, had me inhaling every word. My emotions were so high on this journey that I enjoyed every second of it. The chemistry between Emma and Carter is quite frankly so intense I felt every ounce of it. My pulse raced when Emma’s did because Carter’s presence is just so all encompassing, I mean, how you could function when this hot, intense and dangerous man traps you with just a look? Well….I was a goner no doubt about it, my face flushed and I got all tingly, he only had to enter a room or give someone a look and I went all swoony! He was a killer. A ghost in the shadows who was trained to pure perfection. The cold killer. GAH!! I want to go re-read some scenes now!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>“A different look settled over him, a cold mask covered his face. He was no longer the Carter I knew, the one who held me and kissed me. This was the one who killed, and as that sunk in, everything changed. Time slowed until every second passed in rhythm with my heartbeat.”</i>
</b> – Emma<br><br>As for Emma, I really loved her character too. She was so very vulnerable because of her childhood and what had happened to her brother. Then she goes and commits the ultimate crime but with the purest of intentions setting up the story when she runs to find Carter Reed afterwards.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I have been protecting you since you were a child, Emma. I’m not going to stop now.”</i>
</b> – Carter<br><br>Now, despite this vulnerability, Emma had pure strength, she’s a survivor. Yes she felt guilt and conflicted emotions over the sudden path her life has taken, but in a situation where a loved one is threatened, this girl does not hesitate. She pulls her big girlie knickers on and gets the job done. There was nothing weak, annoying or needy about her. Brilliant heroine that’s for sure!<br><br><b>
  <i>“Four days ago, I thought my life was ending. Everything had taken a 180 degree turn.”</i>
</b> – Emma<br><br><b>
  <i>“You’re different Ems. We can’t be normal. You’re not normal anymore. I think what you did changed you too…It’s like a part of you died.”</i>
</b> – Amanda<br><br><b>Jenny:</b> I agree. I could re-read some of those scenes in a heartbeat and Emma was indeed a kick ass heroine. I loved the storyline, I loved the characters, the secondary characters added so much to the story and I was completely bowled over by this authors writing style. I really don’t know what else I can say about this book without prattling on forever. Definitely a favourite of 2013. You know that feeling when a book is coming to an end and you’re torn between racing to finish and trying to savour every single delicious, heart stomping moment? Well, yeah, that me with Carter Reed. I was dreading coming to the end because I knew I would want more and I did! An absolute winner! I LOVED IT! How would you sum this one up G? Hmmm do you think we should include the text messages we were sending whilst we were reading?<br><br><b>
  <i>“You’re mine, Emma. You always have been. I won’t let you go.”</i>

The storyline, the characters and the emotions that I felt whilst reading. The writing was spot on and I’ve got no complaints whatsoever except I just didn’t want it to end and I was gutted to leave Carter behind. Mind you there’s no chance of him ever leaving my heart because he sure made his mark on me!<br><br><b>
  <i>“This,” he growled in a whisper against my lips. “This is what I wanted that night. I couldn’t contain myself and I had to taste you, but tonight is the night I really have you. You’re mine, Emma. You always have been.”</i>

<div id="review_722013198" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/722013198" />
    <a title="Zakirrah BookBlogger" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15894726-zakirrah-bookblogger"><img alt="Zakirrah BookBlogger" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396291066p2/15894726.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/722013198?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zakirrah BookBlogger" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zakirrah BookBlogger" href="/user/show/15894726-zakirrah-bookblogger">Zakirrah BookBlogger</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15894726-zakirrah-bookblogger?shelf=blog-tour">blog-tour</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15894726-zakirrah-bookblogger?shelf=arc-or-netgalley">arc-or-netgalley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer722013198" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer419578545711144813"><b>"You're mine, Emma. You always have been. I won't let you go.” </b><br/><br/>Fantastic book with a gripping storyline, dark, gritty, filled with action, twists and danger. Sooo to all you action lovers this one is for you! It kinds of has a bit of everything in it, it is hot, heartbreaking, heart racing, action-filled and much more. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436979i/883534._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>What would you do if you caught your roommates boyfriend raping her? What if it was you next? </i><br/><br/>When Emma walks into her apartment having skipped going to the gym her day goes from </span>
  <span id="freeText419578545711144813" style="display:none"><b>"You're mine, Emma. You always have been. I won't let you go.” </b><br><br>Fantastic book with a gripping storyline, dark, gritty, filled with action, twists and danger. Sooo to all you action lovers this one is for you! It kinds of has a bit of everything in it, it is hot, heartbreaking, heart racing, action-filled and much more. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436979i/883534._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>What would you do if you caught your roommates boyfriend raping her? What if it was you next? </i><br><br>When Emma walks into her apartment having skipped going to the gym her day goes from bad to worse.Catching her roommates boyfriend raping her she panics and does something she cant take back.She kills him.<br>The boyfriend is no other than the son of a mobster. She couldnt call the police unless she wanted to be hunted and killed and she coulnt let her roommate/ best friend die in the hands of this monster.So she does what she thinks is best she kills him.<br><br>what would you do if you had the mob looking for you? They would come for you and they would kill you.<br><br>Its kind of a no-win situation either way she would have been hunted and killed so after leaving his body in her apartment she runs with her friend. When panic, fear and paranoia sets in she needs to get help.. fast.<br><br><b>"You don't trust anyone, no one except Carter. Go to Carter. He'll take care of everything. He'll take care of you, Ems. I promise." </b><br><br>With her brothers last words ringing in her ears she sets out to find Carter Reed he is the only one that can help her now.<br>Carter Reed was Emma's brother AJ's best-friend and when AJ was murdered he went on a rampage and killed everyone involved in his death.He turned into a killer, its what he is known for cold-hearted killer but Emma knew him before he changed will he still be willing to help her?<br><br>Carter Reed is bloody HOT! Gorgeous, strong, protective, passionate, dangerous and edge oh whats not to love?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380386678ra/746276.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>It was adorable.<br>Then I grinned to myself. Carter Reed was not adorable. Hot and dangerous, but not adorable.. </b><br><br>I loved how he would do anything for Emma to make sure she is safe and protected. He has always been the protector so having Emma around and her worrying about him is so different. He is broken in more ways than one suffering loss and much more bad things that happened to him in the past he is used to taking care of himself. Being with Emma heals his wounds but will it all work out? How long will he keep her protected?<br><br>Emma has always been alone since she lost her brother AJ and Carter went off killing.She had no one, she has very few friends and its mostly her looking after them. she always needed someone to look after her and Carter does that. Carter fills the gaps, fills the loneliness and makes her feel whole again.<br><br>This is mostly in Emma's POV with small parts in Carter POV. I wanted more of Carter it was like his POVs were randomly placed and short.I would have loved to find out more about him, what he was thinking when they came to his POV is was more of an overall summary it wasn't just his thought you saw what the people around him were thinking too. I some what liked it but I needed more his life was a lot more interesting.<br><br><b>"I've been protecting you since I joined the Mauricio Family. You were why I joined them in the first place."</b><br><br>I was disappointed that there weren't many deep convos between Emma and Carter they didn't discuss the past much , well not his past. I wanted to know sooo much more! I wanted it to be a series because well..I love series and getting to know the characters better.<br>This book needed an epilogue! Unless this is going to turn into a serie? ;) It needed something to round it all off it felt like the book just left you hanging and I was flipping through the pages and thinking..whattt? thats it? nooooooo :( <br>Oh btw did anyone else notice that Emma "gasps" alot? :DD<br><br>Overall this was a great book with some unexpected turns it kept me guessing.Its fast- paced and captivating I was intrigued from the moment I read the synopsis.This is the first Tijan book I have read and well after reading it I will be checking out her other books! <br><br><b>**ARC provided by the author for an honest review**<br><br>Check out my blog for more reviews!<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://zakirrahsbookblog.blogspot.co.uk/">http://zakirrahsbookblog.blogspot.co.uk/</a><br><br>Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Zakirr">https://www.facebook.com/pages/Zakirr</a>...<br><br></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="419578545711144813" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

Now he is a dangerous professional badass that made a huge fortune working to the mafia. He’s powerful, everyone’s afraid of him and he decides that he’s going to save Emma. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381509389ra/4960376.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Not only because she was her best-friend little sister, but also because for a long time they were his only family and he always had feelings for her. <br>And her for him, so yeah, you know where this is going.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381509389ra/4960377.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(There’s actually no need for these gifs. I was not particularly fan of Tijan (I mean, Fallen Crest High is a pretty good book, but not a life-changing one.), but she really set the pace on this one. <br>It is hot, sweet, STEAMY with lots of action and killing and extremely well written.<br>If you’re into books that will grab you from page one and not let you do anything else before finishing it, with very cool characters and an awesome story line, well… you better read this one. </span>

<div id="review_715554826" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/715554826" />
    <a title="Andreea Pop" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4858513-andreea-pop"><img alt="Andreea Pop" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486663526p2/4858513.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/715554826?book_show_action=true">Sep 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Andreea Pop" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Andreea Pop" href="/user/show/4858513-andreea-pop">Andreea Pop</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=non-fantasy">non-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=bat-shit-crazy">bat-shit-crazy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=annoying-heroine">annoying-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=real-life-problems">real-life-problems</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=dark-atmosphere">dark-atmosphere</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=never-again">never-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=wth-god-no">wth-god-no</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer715554826" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4575717097852780419">Andreea is not impressed. Andreea is fucking angry, disappointed and downright frustrated. <br/><br/><a href='http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ts7WHLGHNMQ/U_SiJQTc4tI/AAAAAAAAORA/s8LWA1HRLIc/s1600/754312.gif' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408541502ra/10862050.gif' height='167' width='320' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>What's up with that rating average? And how is it possible that this book has so many 5-star reviews that fangirl over the awesomeness that is <i>Carter Reed</i>? I wanted to be one of those fangirls that couldn't stop gushing about it, but I ended up wondering <b>IF I EVEN READ THE SAME BOOK</b>. Prepare for a lot of shouty capitals, ranting and exasperating quotes. Bare with me here, because I might need therapy. </span>
  <span id="freeText4575717097852780419" style="display:none">Andreea is not impressed. Andreea is fucking angry, disappointed and downright frustrated. <br><br><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ts7WHLGHNMQ/U_SiJQTc4tI/AAAAAAAAORA/s8LWA1HRLIc/s1600/754312.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408541502ra/10862050.gif" height="167" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>What's up with that rating average? And how is it possible that this book has so many 5-star reviews that fangirl over the awesomeness that is <i>Carter Reed</i>? I wanted to be one of those fangirls that couldn't stop gushing about it, but I ended up wondering <b>IF I EVEN READ THE SAME BOOK</b>. Prepare for a lot of shouty capitals, ranting and exasperating quotes. Bare with me here, because I might need therapy. <br><br><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-bZzq_t4GmYc/U_SiPqSDcZI/AAAAAAAAOR0/F9ErRWAJrkE/s1600/tumblr_inline_mmb2sbQ87c1qz4rgp.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408541813ra/10862103.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Let me give you the main reason why I absolutely hated <i>Carter Reed</i>. The main character, Emma Martins. She was an absolute pain in the ass. My jaw just dropped at just how stupid and dumb she could be. I was at the point where I was praying she was faking it, because I couldn't comprehend someone being so naive and weak. <br><br><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-ZccpOAEd7iA/U_SiJYtO8aI/AAAAAAAAOQ8/IdhD_MIrEZo/s1600/745945.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408541502ra/10862051.gif" height="179" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>“Mike nodded for me to go in so I did.”</i> <b>Oh, you petulant little thing. DO YOU EVEN HAVE A BRAIN?</b><br><br><i>“Who are you texting?”<br>My head jerked up and I almost dropped my phone as Theresa frowned at me. Her eyes fell to my phone and warmth surged to my cheeks as I fumbled to keep my screen hidden. I knew I was redder than red.”</i> <b>Way to keep it cool.</b><br><br><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-9-asZ3NifVw/U_SiLFqBwZI/AAAAAAAAORM/BAD47SkgHoo/s1600/7258487.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408541813ra/10862104.gif" height="160" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>She's so immature that I wanted to smack her upside down, not to mention strangle her when she actually thought she has a say in all that was happening. She really believed she has the right to fucking complain! <b>NEWS FLASH, HONEY</b> -- the Mob is trying to kill you and you wanted protection; now sit on your goddamn butt and don't put yourself in danger just because you feel like it, or because you're "feeling lonely" or because you "need to help" or because you're so childishly stubborn. <b>ARGHHH</b>. <br><br><i>“He spoke to me like I was two.”</i> <b>You are.</b> <br><br><i>“I flushed. I was an idiot sometimes.”</i> No, you're <b>always</b> an idiot.<br><br><i>“I’m sorry. I wasn’t thinking.”</i> <b>Damn right, you weren't. You have no idea what thinking feels like.</b><br><br><i>“I don’t want to stay away,” I mumbled. I felt ridiculous.”</i> <b>You are that as well.</b> <br><br><i>“I wasn’t helpless and he needed to start telling me what was going on. This was my life too.”</i> <b>Tell that to the priest.</b><br><br><i>“Warmth burst inside of me, but I tried to tone it down. I was becoming one of those gushy types. I hated those types, but I whispered back, “I’m glad you’re coming back.”</i> <b>Hy-po-crite.</b><br><br><i>“I didn’t know what was going on, but I knew he was going to leave me there. Something came up and he needed to handle whatever it was, but I didn’t want to be left behind.”</i> <br><br><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-VsvK3JVZ90s/U_SiNO7afMI/AAAAAAAAORk/Q4CLm0OoNqE/s1600/tumblr_inline_mhjx9iBj6d1r6h22v.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408541813ra/10862105.gif" height="145" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>STOP WHINING!!!</b> <br><br>I might add that she’s also shallow and self-centered:<br><br><i>“My eyes went wide. She downgraded? I could never afford a place like this, not with the salary I earned as Mr. Hudson’s assistant. Then I comprehended the rest of what she had said. “Oh, I’m so sorry about your parents.”</i> <b>Nice save, dumbass.</b> <br><br>Emma resembled a two-year old. At least mentally speaking, because physically she had the body of a horny teenager bimbo in the making. <br>She's trapped in her own little world and she barely talks. Everyone throws questions at her and they're left unanswered because it seems she doesn't have the normal capability of having a conversation.<br><br><b>Proof #1:</b><br><br><i>“What?” Carter looked at me.<br>I must’ve made some sound. “Oh, it’s nothing.” It wasn’t worth talking about.<br>He reached for my hand again and raised it for a soft kiss. “Emma, tell me.”<br>The knots in my stomach loosened at his touch, but I shook my head. This was embarrassing in a small way. “It’s really nothing.”</i><br><br><b>Proof #2:</b><br><br><i>“He asked, “What happened?”<br>I sighed. He always knew. “Nothing.”<br>“Emma.”<br>“Nothing,” my voice rose.<br>He took my arm and pulled me close. “What happened?”<br>“Nothing.”</i><br><br><b>Proof #3:</b><br><br><i>“Emma?”<br>I became aware of his voice. The phone had fallen into the covers and I grabbed it. “Sorry.”<br>“Are you okay?”<br>“I’m fine.”<br>“Emma.”<br>“I am,” I rushed out. “When are you coming back?”<br>“I’ll be back tomorrow night.”<br>“Good.” I took a deep breath. “That’s good.”<br>“Are you sure you’re okay?”<br>“I’m good.”</i><br><br><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ek7b1bG5HkQ/U_SiULuXUOI/AAAAAAAAOSI/hp4bvdckw1c/s1600/tumblr_mogivjI7391r4jpeio1_500.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408541502ra/10862052.gif" height="181" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But now that I think about it, she's not just self-centered. She's <i>Carter</i>-centered. Everything comes back to him and it's quite pathetic how easily she falls for him. If she's not over analyzing her decisions (which she should, because they truly suck), then she's fantasizing about Carter. <br><br><i>“I needed Carter. That made sense to me so that’s what I held onto.”</i> <b>Amazing logic, by the way.</b> <br><br><i>“This creature who held my hand was mine, as I was his. I belonged to him and I gasped in silence as I felt his claim sink into my blood. It went deep to the bones. Everything in me belonged to him, and as I followed him through his club, I knew that I was becoming addicted to him.”</i> <b>Fan-tastic, I'm telling you. She barely knows the guy.</b><br><br><i>“That was normal, to indulge after a hard week at work and laugh with your friends over a glass of wine. This was all normal. I could be normal.<br>Carter wasn’t normal, but I couldn’t only have him in my life now.”</i> <b>Why does it all have to come back to him?! <i>Whyyyyy?</i></b><br><br><i>“I had three friends who I considered family, but now it was Carter. It was quickly becoming all about him.”</i> <b>Duh. Obviously.</b><br><br><i>“Twenty-four hours earlier and I would’ve been pleading for her life. She was innocent. She was pure. She meant no harm. But now I had changed. Theresa had become a friend, but everything shifted last night. Carter was my lover. He was my family. He was my only ally. And because of that, because she held a threat to his life, I told him, “I can’t lose you.”</i> <b>Kill me now. Pleeeease, end my mysery.</b><br><br><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-7iNQAiBK8qM/U_SiO17TnDI/AAAAAAAAORs/3U8lVfmxdeM/s1600/tumblr_inline_mibfvrimcL1qz4rgp.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408541813ra/10862106.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Carter (the character) could've been the best thing in this book. But instead of being a great character, he was double-faced and manipulative. I suppose he had his good times and I admired him for his power, confidence and cunning mind, but that didn't balance the fact that he turned into a sappy love struck guy by the end of the book. How he could've fallen in love with the idiot extraordinaire is beyond me. And are you actually trying to tell me he was whipped about Emma all this time and he didn't make a damn move? <b>ARE YOU SHITTING ME?</b> <br><br><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-NhYwuTt-TzQ/U_Slgmj4kHI/AAAAAAAAOSs/h_Zb9fAwcMg/s1600/tumblr_inline_mhjjvhOFYv1qz4rgp.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408542285ra/10862232.gif" height="133" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>“He tilted my head back and pressed a kiss underneath my chin as he murmured, “I have always loved you.” Another kiss. “I will always love you, Emma. There’s been no other for me.” His hand slid to the back of my neck and his lips moved back to mine. “Now, do you love me?”<br>I grinned against him, unable to hold it in. “You know I do.”</i> <b>I just threw up in my mouth a bit.</b><br><br>Another thing that dumbfounded me was how Emma kept whining about Carter's new demeanor towards her and how <i>"he's not the same Carter anymore."</i> Well, no shit, Sherlock. He joined the <b>FREAKING MOB</b>. What the heck would you expect? Rainbows and sunshine coming out of his ass?! Ugh. <br><br>The secondary characters were flat, undeveloped and plain stupid -- damn, it's like they take life advice from each other. I couldn't connect with any of them. Ben -- infuriatingly dumb and a complete wacko. Theresa -- too quirky and judgemental. Noah -- he sounded like an insecure thirteen year old most of the time. Amanda -- a ridiculous excuse for a friend, but I grew to tolerate her. Mallory -- amazingly naive if she thought having a boyfriend as dangerous as hers would leave her unscathed. <br><br><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-irpbDJrQ2PI/U_SiU9v3d2I/AAAAAAAAOSU/Abbl_uFNSgE/s1600/untitledh.png" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408541502i/10862053.png" height="166" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>“You’re not here trying to get her money, are you?”</i> <b>Great ice-breaker.</b><br><br>This is my first book by Tijan and I seriously hope it's her worst one, because otherwise, if it's one of her great stuff, I'm bound to swear off any other stories she's created. The writing style is, simply put, bad. There are so many repetitive sequences and cringe-worthy lines. I don't know, maybe being inside Emma's brain (small as a pea) triggered my need to turn back to basic second-grade understanding skills, but I doubt that this whole issue couldn't have been avoided my some spot-on editing. I bet the book would've been half its current size and maybe I would've granted another star to my rating. Maybe. <br><br><i>“He didn’t like it. It happened too fast for his liking.”</i> <br><br><i>“I just admitted to myself that there was something between us. I sucked in my breath and my hands started to tremble. My stomach churned and formed knots, but I had to admit that something was growing between Carter and me.”</i> <br><br>Seriously, it's like I'm double reading <b>everything</b>. <br><br><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-eJzQaA2nZBs/U_SiLDF2WrI/AAAAAAAAORU/RwqzWq7_5Gk/s1600/6216771.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408541502ra/10862054.gif" height="179" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I wanted this story to be thrilling and romantic, but it was neither. The premise had so much potential for an action-driven plot, when in reality the story unfolded at a slow pace, with a few bang bang scenes thrown at random to ensure that we haven't forgotten this book is about the Mob. <b>I WAS BORED.</b> Actually, let me say it again:<br><br><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-cLPw6X9y-D8/U_SiRNUH60I/AAAAAAAAOR8/hggxuw0W8lI/s1600/tumblr_inline_mqe9atI26p1qz4rgp.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408541813ra/10862107.gif" height="230" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I was stuck inside Emma's insipid thoughts and the sexy times between her and Carter, although they got me a bit hot and bothered, were vomit inducing after a while because of how unrealistic the chemistry was. <br><br><i>“There were a few more that I didn’t know about until later, but I still killed them. I killed all of them. For you.”</i> <b>How romantic.</b><br><br>I hoped I'd be able to love this book so much, but instead I hated it. I'm not one to bash someone's work and I'm usually really indulgent when it comes to books. I overlook a lot for the sake of enjoying a story, but when it's this horrendous I have to acknowledge that this book wasn't for me. In the beginning, I entertained the idea that I'll give it a 4 stars rating. Then it dropped to 3. Then to 2. And now to 1. <i>*sigh*</i> It's my first one star rating and I'm sad to give it to <i>Carter Reed</i>, but it still doesn't change the fact that I want to throw it out the window even after I finished it.<br><br><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ParZxQuPhzg/U_SiLRJlSHI/AAAAAAAAORQ/YeQGtqQWtaA/s1600/10676542.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408541813ra/10862108.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Carter Reed</i> turns out to be my biggest literary disappointment <b>EVER</b>. I was sure I was going to love it because it had all the right ingredients, but then I actually read it and I'm now left here with a severe headache (I think even my brain is hurting), countless highlighted quotes to account for my dislike and a general impression of <b>WHAT THE ACTUAL FUCK?!</b> If the book got a bunch of serious editing and Emma a personality change, this book would've been ten times better. If. <br><br>I'd say <b>ENJOY!</b> but I don't really recommend it, so...<br><br><b>P.S.:</b> This is my Carter. Pretty good eye candy, don’t you think? <br><br><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-gIVR4rIB1GM/U_SiGYumYlI/AAAAAAAAOQ0/n9QYOAY09BA/s1600/Carter.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408541502i/10862055._SY540_.jpg" height="320" width="240" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="4575717097852780419" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

I would declare war for you.”</b><br><br><br>They have known each other since they were children he was her brother's best friend. However it's been years since she's seen the enigmatic Carter. What will happen, will he help her, will he protect her?!?!?!?!?!!?<br><br><br><b>Well YEA....DUH!!!!!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385510704ra/7163874.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>“I have been protecting you since you were a child, Emma. I’m not going to stop now.”</b><br><br><br><b>
  <u>My thoughts</u>
</b><br><br><br>Wellllllllllll.....I think this could of been magnificent!!! Now don't get me wrong I did enjoy it but I wanted to FEEL it and I didn't quite get there. I needed or wanted to see more of Carter's ruthless side, I wanted him to bring the THUNDER...all that badassness...I wanted him unleashed!!! <b> YUMMMMM!!</b> I mean it happened a couple times but I would of liked more!!! I'm <b>GREEDY</b> what can I say!!!<br><br><br>I would of also liked for Emma to be more sure of herself but her character basically stayed consistent so I was ok with her in the end.....other than I think she's a bitch because, well, she got Carter Reed!!! Damn her:))))<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385511327i/7163987.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So to sum it up I wanted to see more of Carter and get in his head...we got a few chapters in his POV but there should of been MORE!!! LOVED LOVED his character!!!!<br><br>This author is fantastic......I have liked every book by her so FAR!!!!!<br><br><br>I may add more to this but this is all for now:)<br></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1137847673" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1137847673?book_show_action=true">Dec 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Jennifer by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1137847673" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1882957587122416523"><b>
  <i>”I would declare war for you.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419249083ra/13020523.gif' width='390' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>This story started off with a bang but thereafter was missing something. Perhaps a better back story or Carter's pov from the past? The I love Yous felt like they were out of nowhere for where these two were and are with one another. It could be that added depth from the characters was needed but I just wasn’t connected with the two main characters in the slightest. <br/><br/>Emma is on the run after killing a mobster and goes to her deceased brother’s best friend Carter</span>
  <span id="freeText1882957587122416523" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>”I would declare war for you.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419249083ra/13020523.gif" width="390" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>This story started off with a bang but thereafter was missing something. Perhaps a better back story or Carter's pov from the past? The I love Yous felt like they were out of nowhere for where these two were and are with one another. It could be that added depth from the characters was needed but I just wasn’t connected with the two main characters in the slightest. <br><br>Emma is on the run after killing a mobster and goes to her deceased brother’s best friend Carter Reed for protection. Sadly, I found the story boring in parts compared to the other books I have read by this author but I read on to see how things would play out. Overall this was an okay read for me.<br><br><b>Thank you Bev for the gift!! </b><br></span>

<div id="review_692482166" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/692482166" />
    <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time"><img alt="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460037460p2/9072385.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/692482166?book_show_action=true">Aug 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="user" itemprop="url" name="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time">*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>
