        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer692482166" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16698482821380349606">4.5--<b>I Couldn't Stop Reading</b>--Stars!!!<br/><br/>This one really starts with a bang!! *pun intended* Emma walks in on her roomate Mallory getting raped by her boyfriend with mafia connections and decides to take matters in to her own hands. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380734902ra/3116536.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Freaking out and on the run, Emma and her roomate Mallory end up at their friend Ben's house. Trying to find a way out the mess, Emma turns to Carter Reed...childhood friend, BFF to her dead brother AJ and aka The Cold Killer. Carter Reed has his own mafia ties....to th</span>
  <span id="freeText16698482821380349606" style="display:none">4.5--<b>I Couldn't Stop Reading</b>--Stars!!!<br><br>This one really starts with a bang!! *pun intended* Emma walks in on her roomate Mallory getting raped by her boyfriend with mafia connections and decides to take matters in to her own hands. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380734902ra/3116536.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Freaking out and on the run, Emma and her roomate Mallory end up at their friend Ben's house. Trying to find a way out the mess, Emma turns to Carter Reed...childhood friend, BFF to her dead brother AJ and aka The Cold Killer. Carter Reed has his own mafia ties....to the rival mafia family.<br><br>Carter Reed:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380734902ra/3116537.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Can I just say, I <b>LOVED</b> Carter! From the moment Emma seeks him out he goes balls to the wall to protect her. And finding out he's been protecting her and watching out for her this whole time...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/666302.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don't even know what else to say about this book....other than I literally could not stop reading. Emma becoming entwined with Carter and his lifestyle. Carter trying to protect Emma from the lingering threats.....can Carter protect her? What will happen to her friends? I had to know how it was going to all play out. <br><br>I think my ONLY complaint about the book would be that the sex is somewhat fade to black. The sexual chemistry and tension between Carter and Emma was definitely HOT but when it came time to actually doing the deed I wish it would have been a bit more descriptive....especially with a protective, alpha male like Carter. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380423038ra/842483.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I also just want to thank Tijan for writing a standalone book. I'm a huge Tijan fan but she likes to write the series....and normally she jumps from series to series. So I was so happy that this was a standalone. And that cover.....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380734902ra/3116538.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380734902ra/3116539.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Read it and love it people!!! </span>

<div id="review_730676874" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/730676874" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/730676874?book_show_action=true">Sep 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=6-stars-top-favorites">6-stars-top-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=5-stars-favorites">5-stars-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer730676874" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3525807350230650606"><b>Excerpt and more posted <a href='http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com/2013/10/carter-reed-by-tijan.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>HERE</a></b><br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/YNoxxCd' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381589038i/5071682._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>5 Dangerous Stars</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Carter was lethal. His body was craved and molded to perfection.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>I loved Carter Reed. From start to finish, it was everything I look for in an alpha-damsel-in-distress read. If you like what I like, then you will love this book. It’s also has the same feel to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/639161773' rel='nofollow noopener'>Killing Sarai</a> (to me at least)<br/><br/><b>NOW, I have to put that big fat Disclaimer</b> - > This book has received a lot of 4 star reviews. Let me tell you why this book isn’t a home run for ever</span>
  <span id="freeText3525807350230650606" style="display:none"><b>Excerpt and more posted <a href="http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com/2013/10/carter-reed-by-tijan.html" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a></b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/YNoxxCd" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381589038i/5071682._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>5 Dangerous Stars</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Carter was lethal. His body was craved and molded to perfection.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I loved Carter Reed. From start to finish, it was everything I look for in an alpha-damsel-in-distress read. If you like what I like, then you will love this book. It’s also has the same feel to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/639161773" rel="nofollow noopener">Killing Sarai</a> (to me at least)<br><br><b>NOW, I have to put that big fat Disclaimer</b> - &gt; This book has received a lot of 4 star reviews. Let me tell you why this book isn’t a home run for everyone. I LOVE damsel in distress books and Emma isn’t the strongest heroine, but I love her. Read the blurb and read the reviews. You will know if this is right for you.<br><br>Emma witnesses her roommate getting raped and she kills the attacker. The attacker happens to be a part of the mob. Emma can’t go to the cops and she knows it’s only a matter of time before she will be killed. She goes to Carter Reed to help her. Carter is the best friend of Emma’s brother and she hasn’t seen Carter in ten years. Carter Reed isn’t the same boy she remembers growing up with, but she needs someone to protect her.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/KvAhYgF" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381589038i/5071683._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>No other man had made me feel as he had and being back at Octave opened the floodgates. I wanted him even more.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>First off, I picked up this book because of two things, Tijan and the cover. Yeah, cover snob, whatever, but that’s me. Then I read the blurb and I was like oh yeah. The book starts off with a HUGE BANG, it’s kind of slap-you-in-face kind of thing and it’s good. You slowly form a relationship with Emma and kind of get to know her as a character. She’s a little stubborn, wish-washy, but really loyal and determined. I usually don’t like wish washy girls, but it adds tension to the story.<br><br><b>And of course the reason for the whole book. Mr. SEXY CARTER REED. SWOON Major overload. I love him, I want him and damn.</b> He’s a book boyfriend and lord, I have a major crush on him. I know, I’m getting carried away, but you get the point. He’s a killer and a brute, what more could you ask for? I like everything about his character, from his past hardships, how he handles tough situations and the way he reacts to Emma. You will love him, I promise.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/POyKZDM" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381589038i/5071684.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>His eyes were dark with lust and need. I knew he saw the same in me, but I didn’t care any longer. I needed him…<br><br>No matter what path Carter would take us, I’d go with him. I was becoming him… I’d always follow.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Carter Reed has some fast pace moments, but mostly there’s a lot of character and story development. There aren’t any flash-backs and there are bits of Carter’s POV sprinkled in, which I really liked. Mostly, it’s a book about a girl in trouble and she seeks help. There are a lot of obstacles and things thrown at Emma and Carter to keep you on your toes. The story isn’t really steamy, yes there are some nice parts, but you can tell it’s not a major focal point, but there is plenty of sexual tension.<br><br>There isn’t an epilogue, which doesn’t bother me, but I know a lot of readers like it, but there is an ending. For now, it’s a standalone novel, but I cross my fingers that Tijan will write a second book and make it a series.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18221931.Carter_Reed__Carter_Reed___1_" title="Carter Reed (Carter Reed, #1) by Tijan" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1376139745s/18221931.jpg" alt="Carter Reed (Carter Reed, #1) by Tijan" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://amzn.to/1Ed3bZ1" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a> 99 CENTS SALE</span>
  <a data-text-id="3525807350230650606" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_729172039" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/729172039" />
    <a title="*on hiatus*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5058045-on-hiatus"><img alt="*on hiatus*" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/729172039?book_show_action=true">Sep 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="*on hiatus*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="*on hiatus*" href="/user/show/5058045-on-hiatus">*on hiatus*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058045-on-hiatus?shelf=mafia">mafia</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058045-on-hiatus?shelf=is-this-over-yet">is-this-over-yet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058045-on-hiatus?shelf=too-predictable">too-predictable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058045-on-hiatus?shelf=tstl-heroine">tstl-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058045-on-hiatus?shelf=i-don-t-get-the-hype">i-don-t-get-the-hype</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058045-on-hiatus?shelf=not-as-good-as-blurb">not-as-good-as-blurb</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058045-on-hiatus?shelf=what-was-i-thinking">what-was-i-thinking</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058045-on-hiatus?shelf=meh">meh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058045-on-hiatus?shelf=waste-of-time">waste-of-time</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer729172039" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11966729685864613400"><b> 2.5 stars </b><br/><br/>Oh... why?? Why?? Did I have to jump on the Carter Reed bandwagon just because I saw somewhere that a sequel was coming up soon? I steered clear of this book when it first came out two years ago, despite all the hype because my gut kept telling me to stay away.<br/><br/>Now two years later, my reckless, impressionable self throws herself all in, without bothering to check any reviews first and judge whether it was going to be worth my while. <br/><br/>Well, in short, this book was just... weird... <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416014589ra/11877038.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The st</span>
  <span id="freeText11966729685864613400" style="display:none"><b> 2.5 stars </b><br><br>Oh... why?? Why?? Did I have to jump on the Carter Reed bandwagon just because I saw somewhere that a sequel was coming up soon? I steered clear of this book when it first came out two years ago, despite all the hype because my gut kept telling me to stay away.<br><br>Now two years later, my reckless, impressionable self throws herself all in, without bothering to check any reviews first and judge whether it was going to be worth my while. <br><br>Well, in short, this book was just... weird... <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416014589ra/11877038.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story started out pretty ok, standard contrived clichéd story about this chick who is forced to commit a crime and seek help from the uber powerful, dangerous, panty-melting mob dude. Ok, I can roll with that. <br><br>But I think what really threw me off was the writing. It wasn't descriptive enough. It felt jumpy, amateurish and as deep and complex as a two by four. You know what kind of writing it is? That ham-fisted kind that begs you, just begs you to SEE THINGS THE AUTHORS WAY. SEE, CARTER REED IS OH SO HOT, OH SO DANGEROUS, I'M TOO LAZY TO SHOW YOU WHY OR HOW, JUST BELIEVE MEEEE!! SEE EVERYBODY WANTS TO HUMP HIM, AND LOOK... GUNS! AND A SHIT-TON OF GUARDS WITH EAR PIECES. HE'S OH SO WRONG, BUT OH SO RIGHT. HE'S A KILLER BUT MY PANTIES MELT. And if I read about this chick's throbbing lady bits one more time I was going to murder my perfectly nice new iPhone 6+ and for that I would have hated this author for-the-fuck-ever. I was confused about why people seemed to say such random things. I was confused about locations, spaces, people's ages, looks, occupations, Emma's bitchiness. It was all so odd.<br><br>Halfway through the book that sinking feeling of dread bloomed fully and I realized just how little I gave a damn for any of these characters. Emma annoyed me with her melodramatics, there were too many seemingly useless secondary characters. Theresa was all over the place and seemed psycho to me. I expected her to end up being a killer but alas, nothing that interesting happened. She was just this weird as hell character that served no real interesting purpose. And WTF with Amanda, I mean what was the point of all these people? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412098161ra/11323752.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If this author had spent a little more time putting Carter on the page instead of weird-shady Theresa, this would have been much more interesting. Also, the insta-lust and insta-love are pretty heavy in this book. You get cheated out of a true organic development of the story because it turns out <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They've known each other for years because he was her brother's best friend and he's been watching her all this time and he's always loved her <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Yeah, right. *rolls eyes* I didn't feel the love declarations. In fact I didn't feel anything while reading this book except a boredom edging on desperation. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1430242889ra/14697280.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As for the POVs, what the hell was that? It was so jarring to switch between Emma's first person POV to Carter's 3rd person POV. Why couldn't she keep the POVs consistent? It made Carter seem more remote and it seemed to serve no real purpose. <br><br>Despite this rant, this book was semi-decent, in that I didn't have any humongous issues that would prevent me from recommending it. It was absolutely not my cup of tea and it's the perfect example of what I've become to dread in the romance genre: An over-hyped, mediocre book with a flimsy, contrived plot, underdeveloped characters and a cheesy underlining. Having said that, if you loved this one, I'm happy for you and it's no negative reflection on you. This is just my sincere opinion. I thought it was irritatingly mediocre. A much better book that this really reminded me of was Crow's Row by Julie Hockley.<br><br>I have a horrible track record with mafia books. I've only loved the Evan Arden series by Shay Savage (GENIUS and amazingly done male POV) And Sempre by JM Darhower (very romantic). So I'm rapidly losing faith in this mob enforcer, mob killer, assassin, mafia romance genre. I hope something else comes along that makes me change my mind. <br><br>I was so glad when this book was over I literally sighed and said FINALLY!!! <br><br>2.5 stars. <br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="11966729685864613400" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_695364998" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/695364998" />
    <a title="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11672704-donna-the-romance-cover"><img alt="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1369044455p2/11672704.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/695364998?book_show_action=true">Aug 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" href="/user/show/11672704-donna-the-romance-cover">Donna ~ The Romance Cover</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer695364998" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17140230763942013132">Carter Reed by Tijan<br/><br/>5 stars!!<br/><br/><br/><b>“This,” he growled in a whisper against my lips. “This is what I wanted that night. I couldn’t help myself and I had to taste you, but tonight is the night I really have you. You’re mine, Emma. You always have been.”</b><br/><br/><br/>Tijan has done it again, this author has never failed me. I absolutely loved this book and I absolutely adore Carter Reed. Seriously, you could not help but fall in love with this man.<br/><br/>Emma has been on her own for a while, when she was younger she was shuf</span>
  <span id="freeText17140230763942013132" style="display:none">Carter Reed by Tijan<br /><br />5 stars!!<br /><br /><br /><b>“This,” he growled in a whisper against my lips. “This is what I wanted that night. I couldn’t help myself and I had to taste you, but tonight is the night I really have you. You’re mine, Emma. You always have been.”</b><br /><br /><br />Tijan has done it again, this author has never failed me. I absolutely loved this book and I absolutely adore Carter Reed. Seriously, you could not help but fall in love with this man.<br /><br />Emma has been on her own for a while, when she was younger she was shuffled from foster home to foster home but she always had her brother AJ for company. Unfortunately, AJ became embroiled with the mob and was murdered for his troubles so Emma had to quickly adapt to being alone. For years she had got on with her life and was doing really well for herself. She had a flat with a girlfriend and a good job.<br /><br />One night that all changed and Emma would be forever worrying about her actions, she was scared and alone and was panicking. What should she do, should she run, stay, fight or die even?? Sounds melodramatic but once you read and see what her situation is, you become frightened for her. One thing that keeps coming to the forefront of her thoughts was something her brother said.<br /><br /><b>“No matter who knocks on the door, you don’t answer it. You don’t trust anyone, no one except Carter. Go to Carter. He’ll take care of you, Ems. I promise.”</b><br /><br />Emma knew Carter from when she was younger, she had secretly crushed on the guy for as long as she could remember but he was AJ’s best friend, but more like a brother. When they were in foster care he was always with them, they were inseperable. But she was so wary, he was well known, he had worked his way up the ranks in the mob and was a force to be reckoned with. He was intimidating, people ran when he walked in a room, but he was extremely resourceful, powerful and a well respected business man…but mostly, he was extremely hot!! Smoking hot!! Pantie combusting, smoking hot!! Emma had always felt a connection to him but it was something that was never acted upon and she was wary of being able to cope with seeing him again.<br /><br /><b>“I know who you are, Carter. I’m the only one who knows you.”</b><br /><br />Carter Reed oozes sex appeal, he is extremely good looking, well built and ripped (he is a trained fighter). He is also extremely private. He knows he draws attention but tries to slink into the background...he doesn’t want to be noticed. He is dangerous, he is cool and he is calculating, he doesn’t have a conscience and he only has one Achilles Heel…Emma! Carter has always loved and wanted Emma, but he needed her to want him, he was a patient man, he would bide his time. He knew that she was the one for him and was willing to wait. He knew the day would come and now that she had come to him, he was not willing to let her go.<br /><br /><b>“I have always loved you.” Another kiss. “I will always love you, Emma. There’s no other for me.”</b><br /><br />I can’t say too much about the story as it would spoil it and this is one of those books that you have to start and savour for yourself. Tijan has done an amazing job of drawing the reader in and the build up throughout this book is captivating, I could not put it down. The book is packed with emotion, you will experience it all from anger, fear, angst, passion and love. The chemistry between Carter and Emma is seriously off the charts and it radiates from the page, you are totally sucked in to their relationship and you can’t help but will them on through their battles and their relationship. This was one dynamic duo that I was truly rooting for.<br /><br /><b>“I looked without thinking and was caught by his gaze. He had captured me, my body and mind. As a sob rose in my throat, my body betrayed me. It softened underneath his holds. The fight was leaving me and it was being replaced with desire.”</b><br /><br />I know I have rambled about Carter, well who wouldn’t…he is totally A-MA-ZING!! But I will have to say that Emma is one of the best female leads that I have read about for a long time, she wasn’t whiney, when she had good reason to be., she picked herself up, dusted herself off and went with the flow. No matter what was thrown at her, she dealt and played a blinding hand. It was great to read about such a strong woman. The change in her throughout the book was totally believable, she moulded to her new life brilliantly and seamlessly without moaning. She had a few moments, but that was a minor adjustment.<br /><br />All I can say is Carter, you can watch over me anytime and I really mean anytime!! He has just climbed into my top book boyfriends and I really hope that this is not the end of Carter Reed. I could read about him FOR-EV-ER…I am even willing to beg Tijan for more…(although can you finish Fallen Crest first ;-) I am missing Mason too!!)<br /><br />Amazing book, totally loved it and highly recommended. No woman should go without a bit of Carter Reed in her life!!<br /><br />Phew…seriously…Carter, Carter oi…I’m over here…yes…here!!!<br /><br />Well played Tijan, another fantastic read!<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.theromancecover.com">www.theromancecover.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="17140230763942013132" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1058773129" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1058773129" />
    <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27276528-liz"><img alt="✰ Liz ✰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451097545p2/27276528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1058773129?book_show_action=true">Sep 18, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=alpha-male-love">alpha-male-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1058773129" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1949128783843013515">Carter Reed begins with a bang. It is a book that sucks you in right from the first page and doesn't release it's hold on you until the last word is read. Damn, I love a good book with action, romance, and lots of steam!<br/><br/>Emma comes home and finds her roommate being raped by her so called "boyfriend". Emma is no stranger to violence and she arms herself and takes action.<br/><br/><b>"We should call the police, but no—I had killed someone. No, I had killed Jeremy Dunvan. We couldn’t call anyone."</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418617070i/12849550.jpg' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Emma realizes r</span>
  <span id="freeText1949128783843013515" style="display:none">Carter Reed begins with a bang. It is a book that sucks you in right from the first page and doesn't release it's hold on you until the last word is read. Damn, I love a good book with action, romance, and lots of steam!<br><br>Emma comes home and finds her roommate being raped by her so called "boyfriend". Emma is no stranger to violence and she arms herself and takes action.<br><br><b>"We should call the police, but no—I had killed someone. No, I had killed Jeremy Dunvan. We couldn’t call anyone."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418617070i/12849550.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Emma realizes right away that she is in trouble. She and Mallory run to a friend's apartment. Emma needs help. She remembers that her deceased brother's best friend is very powerful. She can trust him. <br><br><b>“No matter who knocks on the door, you don’t answer it. You don’t trust anyone, no one except Carter. Go to Carter. He’ll take care of everything. He’ll take care of you, Ems. I promise.”</b><br><br>Emma goes to Carter for help.<br><br> <b>Carter</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418617070i/12849551._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Carter was AJ's best friend. Carter is her friend. Carter is also a killer. <br><br> <b>"Carter Reed was a killer. He was connected to the mob. I never knew how important he was to the Mauricio Family, but I knew he was powerful."</b><br><br>Carter doesn't hesitate to take care of Emma. <br><br> <b>“I’ll take care of you.” Relief soared through me and my body gave way. But before I slid to the floor in a crumbled heap again, he caught my arm and hoisted me to his lap." </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402845113i/9995349._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Events move at hyper speed throughout this book. The severity of Emma's situation increases her need for Carter. He makes her feel safe. He takes care of her. He has been taking care of her for many years. Carter has been loving Emma from afar. <br><br><b>“You did all of that for me?” “I would declare war for you.” He stole my breath, again. It was becoming difficult to breathe around this man. I always felt like I was having a heart attack, and this was no exception."</b><br> <br>Overall, I found Carter Reed to be a quick and action packed read. I thoroughly enjoyed the supporting characters and how they played into the story. The build up between Carter and Emma was quick. Because of their previous relationship and history, it doesn't take these two long to connect. Emma needs time to figure out who she is. However, she is sure about her place with Carter. Carter was an amazing hero. He was strong, caring, protective, passionate, loving, and HOT! I highly recommend this book to anyone who enjoys action in their romance books! I sincerely hope there is a follow up for this one!<br><br> <b>"I was weak with too many strong feelings sweeping inside of me, too many and too powerful for me to name, but as I gazed up at him, I saw his strength. As I lay in his arms and as he turned for me once more during the night, our bodies moved together as one and I felt my own strength awaken inside of me. I had grown addicted to this beautiful man. He was mine. I would always love this man."</b><br><br><br><br></span>

  <span id="freeText4887111365991234756" style="display:none">Sometimes I get carried away by all of the excitement generated by status updates. Little teases of quotes from the characters dot my update page calling out to me... “see how that sounds... enticing... sexy... "<br /><br />I will make an instant buy and go for it.<br />This was that type of purchase. The cover was hot.<br />The tease from my friends, more than hot.<br />Click clicked and started the read.<br /><br />My first impression was positive... I was duly shocked by the opening scene. Dramatic things were happening and I got the set up and situation. <br />Yet after the set up; the layout of the story and sense of the main characters, I didn't connect the way I normally do. I understood he was the brooding dark powerful yet broken inside man... but I had wanted more....I wanted more communication; ahmmm like the tease I got on my updates. I wanted a woman equal to match him. I wanted her to be smart and even though the situation she was in was complex, I wanted her to react with more logic and sense. <br />Didn't happen. Not for me, but maybe it will for you.<br /><br />I will still be excited and teased by my updates with my click click finger ready to go :D<br /></span>

<div id="review_725262995" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/725262995" />
    <a title="Geri Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads"><img alt="Geri Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487874758p2/11757728.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/725262995?book_show_action=true">Sep 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Geri Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Geri Reads" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads">Geri Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer725262995" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5373321284002283787"><b>4.5 Carter Reed Stars!</b><br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>"You did all of that for me?"<br/>"I would declare war for you."</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/>I have enjoyed Tijan's stories in the past and this one was no exception. <br/><br/>Just reading from the first chapter alone, I know it's going to be good. The blurb pretty much revealed that. I know going in what was going to happen but boy, the way it was written was just fantastic. Every emotion that Emma was feeling was so tangible. It felt like I was there myself watching all those horrible things as they unfold.<br/><br/>Emm</span>
  <span id="freeText5373321284002283787" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Carter Reed Stars!</b><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"You did all of that for me?"<br>"I would declare war for you."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>I have enjoyed Tijan's stories in the past and this one was no exception. <br><br>Just reading from the first chapter alone, I know it's going to be good. The blurb pretty much revealed that. I know going in what was going to happen but boy, the way it was written was just fantastic. Every emotion that Emma was feeling was so tangible. It felt like I was there myself watching all those horrible things as they unfold.<br><br>Emma came home early only to find her best friend being raped by her douche-bag boyfriend. Emma did what she had to do and killed the bastard in order to save her friend. The only problem was her best friend's boyfriend was the son of a powerful mob boss. So now, Emma, along with her friend was forced to hide knowing that there will surely be retribution for what she has done. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“You don’t trust anyone, no one except Carter. Go to Carter. He’ll take care of everything. He’ll take care of you, Ems. I promise.” – AJ</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Fortunately for Emma, she has someone on her side. Someone who is even more fearsome and more powerful than those who are seeking her life--Carter Reed. Carter Reed grew up with Emma and her older brother AJ. And it was Carter Reed who avenged her brother's death at the hands of the same rival mob and it was Carter Reed who, unbeknownst to Emma, continued to protect her. <br><br>Carter Reed is mysterious, powerful and connected. Emma went to him for protection. For Emma, being with him stirred up memories and feelings she had long since buried. Emma fought against those feelings knowing that Carter is as dangerous as her enemies, if not, even more so because he has the power to hurt her not only physically but emotionally as well. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=ejetqq" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380437443ra/884562.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This book had the right amount of action, drama, betrayal and intrigue. But at the heart of it all is a love story. Carter and Emma. We get some snippets from their children and we get a glimpsed of Carter's childhood and how it affected him. We also get to know Emma's brother through her own memories which pretty much intertwines with Carter's. <br><br>The pacing was great. The characterizations were excellent. And it was definitely one of those books that you shouldn't start at 11 pm because you're going to be up all night finishing it. Some parts are brutal and very difficult to read but still very interesting and very vital to the whole story.<br><br>The secondary characters were brilliantly written. Each of them played vital roles to the story. One thing about Tijan's characters is that you'll never know what they're going to do next. You think you know a character, you like them and then suddenly, boom! They just surprise the heck out of you. Some good and some bad. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/xJn2k74" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430921ra/864288.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The only reason I didn't give this 5 stars is the fact that the ending left me wanting. I wanted more. Yes, there is an HEA but I must admit I wanted a little bit of those cheesy and gooey stuff I call an epilogue. But I have a feeling we're going to see more of Carter and Emma. I certainly want to see them playing a role in Noah and Theresa's story. Assuming there is going to be one. But what the heck! A girl can hope, right?<br><br> <br><i>ARC provided by the author in exchange for an honest review.</i><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="5373321284002283787" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer13603446518859712879"><b>Buddy read with Audrey Thunder</b><br/><br/>Audrey was being coward, she escaped her 'responsibility' to finished this! LOL<br/><br/>Let me tell you this. <br/>During the reading, this main character, Emma, given me a headache. Twice. Twice of migraine.<br/>She was so annoying. Drama queen, too demanding, pushy, and acted like a spoiled little princess when it comes to Carter's "service".<br/>I mean...c'mon...you'd killed people, you abandoned your stressful friends, and let them hunted by the mob, while you're looking for a shelter </span>
  <span id="freeText13603446518859712879" style="display:none"><b>Buddy read with Audrey Thunder</b><br><br>Audrey was being coward, she escaped her 'responsibility' to finished this! LOL<br><br>Let me tell you this. <br>During the reading, this main character, Emma, given me a headache. Twice. Twice of migraine.<br>She was so annoying. Drama queen, too demanding, pushy, and acted like a spoiled little princess when it comes to Carter's "service".<br>I mean...c'mon...you'd killed people, you abandoned your stressful friends, and let them hunted by the mob, while you're looking for a shelter , to another mob. When a mob happened to be your long lost friend of a brother. And after you set eyes on his "perfect GQ profile", you forgot about the murder you've done, and lusting after him. And it seemed that you can't stop your throbbing vagina....for him!<br>That's Emma, everybody.<br><br>Why did I finish this anyway....<b>it's all for Carter</b>, he's a hottie...and I found my self a bit fond of him. Feels like wanted to throw Emma to the gator, and keep him for my self.... <br>#evil woman<br><br>And about Carter? I think he's a lot more nauseated by her. It proved that he's disappeared so many times, even Emma begged him to stay.<br>This mob guy, was just like Bruce Wayne.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380734903i/3116545._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One time he jump in and out the car (at night), and then disappeared a few days (maybe he's hiding in his bat cave? like Audrey told me, gagged him self.....)...and when Emma started to trapped in danger (right, just when she's in danger)...he was just popped...just like that...from Greece, NY, Japan...wherever....just name it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380734903ra/3116546.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380734903ra/3116547.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Don't get me wrong...for a mobster, he's kinda nice guy, he's too lame for someone like him...<br>Even when she pursued him (yup! pursued him!) to say "I love you"....I didn't see one tiny little spark between them. It was just about Emma's hungry vagina. Sigh.<br><br>This can be a good story, if...there's NOT too many confusing scene along the story.<br><br>I dunno...Maybe I'm in minority here....but this book just made me dizzy and frowning all the time...and rolling eyes....and questioning....Really?...Really?...Seriously?<br><br>This one failed me. Really sorry.</span>

<div id="review_707133579" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/707133579" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/707133579?book_show_action=true">Aug 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=read-to-review">read-to-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=pull-out-the-guns-mafia">pull-out-the-guns-mafia</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer707133579" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12097919153958573060">I am in such a blissful book hangover!! This is my fifth book by Tijan and what she promises, she delivers with a bang! It’s been three days since I’ve read it and I couldn’t even bring myself to start another…I’m just <i>so</i> consumed by the characters, the romance, the plot and the setting---> LOVE the whole dangerous, mysterious, sexy mafia background!! Seriously, is there anything this author can’t write?!?! <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434831ra/878068.gif' width='300' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The opening scene literally stole my breath. And not in a “oh my gosh, it’s sooo beautifu</span>
  <span id="freeText12097919153958573060" style="display:none">I am in such a blissful book hangover!! This is my fifth book by Tijan and what she promises, she delivers with a bang! It’s been three days since I’ve read it and I couldn’t even bring myself to start another…I’m just <i>so</i> consumed by the characters, the romance, the plot and the setting---&gt; LOVE the whole dangerous, mysterious, sexy mafia background!! Seriously, is there anything this author can’t write?!?! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434831ra/878068.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The opening scene literally stole my breath. And not in a “oh my gosh, it’s sooo beautiful and swoon-worthy way.” It was <b>intense</b>, it was <b>gritty</b>, it was <b>provocative</b>, and right then and there, my heart went out to Emma. The horrifying scene she took in, the decision she needed to make, and her tenacity and fierceness in handling the situation truly impressed me. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380298611ra/685948.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>With everything to run from and nowhere else to go, Emma turns to her late brother’s best friend Carter Reed, now a wealthy, lethal and powerful man in the mafia family. It’s been ten years since they last met, and Carter has evolved from the sweet, innocent boy he was before. <br><br><i>“He had sculpted his body into a weapon. He had done it on purpose.”<br><br>“Shit. He was perfect. And he was a killer.”</i><br><br><b>Absolutely</b>. But a loyal, passionate, and driven one to be exact. No matter the time, location, or circumstance, his number one priority is Emma, and always has been Emma. <br><br><i>“You did all of that for me?”<br><br>“I would declare war for you.”</i><br><br>The story really is compelling and attention-grabbing, all the way. While some of the events that happened I wasn’t so convinced of its believability, for the most part, the action, the drama, the passion, the angst, I could all <i>feel</i> seep into me. The “mafia intrigue” by itself kept my heart racing throughout the book, and kept me guessing to Emma and Carter’s future. I literally had no idea what was going to happen next, who would (possibly) die, and what the mafia had in store for them. Even Carter didn’t have a firm grasp on their future, but the one thing he knew for certain was his love for Emma, and the lengths he’d go through to protect her. <br><br><i>“And I will always worry, but it’s because I love you. I will never control you, Emma. You can make your own decisions and go where you want and I will never say otherwise. But I need you to know that if I worry about you, it’s because I love you. I want you safe. I will always want you safe, no matter who you are with or what you’re doing.”</i><br><br>I didn’t want to finish this book. I wanted to take my sweet time savoring Tijan’s fluent and seductive writing, but before I knew it, eight hours passed and I was on the final page of Carter Reed. I could probably prattle on and on about all the marvelous qualities this book possesses. No doubt about it, Tijian has always been a 1-click author for me, and Carter Reed, both the book and the man, only cements that fact. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434831ra/878069.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>4.5+ WHAT-AN-ASTOUNDING-THRILL-RIDE STARS!!! <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12097919153958573060" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('dpXlXDSQyWwUZ1v3iWegMZauXgjoVGReuw9Tev0bO9x6q6FGFPjf4+UOb6K7yJzlcBZ/4sbNviBPa8em7Vdh4A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('4R7fuUDQyBeVA94TZpLFJmXKJKYCWq3Wut1kjqRJYKPtIJujYLjemGRq6kZUPfnyg3IFTCzDd6hOufBStAU6nw==')})
  }
